[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNI global refs: [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m, weak refs: [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer timeout occurred during fuzzing of the Apache Commons Compress [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary's TAR archive functionality. The timeout was triggered after approximately [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m seconds of execution, with the main thread consuming significant CPU time [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m25853.[0m[39m85ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while stuck in BigDecimal division operations during PAX header [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing in TarArchiveEntry.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Overview[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a timeout in the libFuzzer testing framework while [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing TAR archive entries. The fuzzer entry point is [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mCompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which instantiates a `TarFile` object [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith fuzzed input data. The execution becomes unresponsive during the parsing of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPAX headers, specifically when processing timestamp values encoded as decimal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Thread State Analysis[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe main thread [0m[1;39m([0m[33mtid[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0x00005569e8783df0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is in a RUNNABLE state and has consumed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25853.[0m[39m85ms of CPU time out of the [0m[1;36m27.62[0m[39m seconds elapsed. The thread dump shows it [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis actively executing, not blocked or waiting, indicating a computational [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance issue rather than a deadlock or resource contention problem.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe problematic call stack reveals the following execution path:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: `[0m[1;35mCompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` creates a new [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarFile` instance[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **TAR Processing**: `TarFile` constructor initiates TAR entry parsing via [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mgetNextTarEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **PAX Header Handling**: `[0m[1;35mpaxHeaders[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mapplyPaxHeadersToCurrentEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocess extended PAX headers[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Header Update**: `[0m[1;35mupdateEntryFromPaxHeaders[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mprocessPaxHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` parse [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindividual PAX header fields[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Timestamp Parsing**: `[0m[1;35mparseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` converts decimal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimestamp strings to Instant objects[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **BigDecimal Operations**: The execution gets stuck in `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich involves:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.divideAndRemainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.divideToIntegralValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.divide[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operations[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.divideAndRound[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.createAndStripZerosToMatchScale[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Low-Level Division**: Eventually reaching `[0m[1;35mBigInteger.divideAndRemainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `[0m[1;35mMutableBigInteger.divideKnuth[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, with the timeout occurring at [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mMutableBigInteger.divideOneWord[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis appears to be a **denial of service [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability** caused by [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithmic complexity issues. The vulnerability is triggered through crafted input[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat causes excessive computational load during timestamp parsing operations, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to timeout conditions that could be exploited to make the application [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munresponsive.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Deep Mathematical Operations**: The stack trace shows the code is deeply [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested in Java's BigDecimal and BigInteger mathematical operations, specifically in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Knuth division algorithm implementation.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **PAX Header Processing**: The issue occurs during PAX [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPortable Archive [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInterchange Format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m header parsing, which is an extended TAR format that supports [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madditional metadata including high-precision timestamps.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Timestamp Conversion**: The `[0m[1;35mparseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconverting decimal second representations to Instant objects, which involves [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBigDecimal remainder and division operations that can be computationally expensive [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith certain inputs.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Thread Blocking**: All other threads in the system are in normal states [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwaiting, timed waiting, or running compiler/GC tasks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, confirming this is not a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msynchronization or resource contention issue.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **CPU-Bound Operation**: The high CPU consumption [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m25853.[0m[39m85ms in [0m[1;36m27.[0m[39m62s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates the thread is actively computing rather than being blocked.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo fully understand this issue, the following components should be investigated:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m277[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The method [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresponsible for parsing decimal timestamp strings and converting them to Instant [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobjects. Understanding what input format can cause expensive BigDecimal operations [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis critical.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.processPaxHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1603[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The method that processes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindividual PAX headers and delegates to parsing methods. Review the validation and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitization of PAX header values.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateEntryFromPaxHeaders[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1946[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The method that [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplies PAX headers to the current entry. Check if there are any limits or [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstraints on header values.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mTarFile.paxHeaders[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m605[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;35mTarFile.applyPaxHeadersToCurrentEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m326[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The methods that [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morchestrate PAX header processing. Investigate if there are size limits or [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation checks for PAX headers.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Input validation mechanisms**: Review whether there are any limits on the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision, scale, or magnitude of decimal values that can be provided in PAX [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheaders, particularly for timestamp fields.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **BigDecimal usage patterns**: Examine how BigDecimal objects are constructed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand used in the timestamp parsing code, particularly regarding scale and precision [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msettings that could impact performance.[0m                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"https[0m[32m://bugs.openjdk.org/browse/JDK-6560193"[0m[39m>JDK-[0m[1;36m6560193[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m><[0m[35m/[0m[95mli[0m[39m>[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:            <li [0m[33mid[0m[39m=[0m[32m"Ref[0m[32m-1-24-5"[0m[39m>[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m][0m[39m: <a [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"https[0m[32m://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?[0m[32mname[0m[32m=[0m[32mCVE[0m[32m-2012-2098"[0m[39m>CVE-[0m[1;36m2012[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2098[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95ma[0m[39m><[0m[35m/[0m[95mli[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:          <[0m[35m/[0m[95mul[0m[39m>[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:          <p>Only applications using CompressorStreamFactory class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mauto-detection of file types[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, TarArchiveInputStream and TarFile [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:             classes to parse TAR files are impacted. Since this code was [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced in v1.[0m[1;36m22[0m[39m, only that version and later versions are impacted.<[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:        <[0m[35m/[0m[95msubsection[0m[39m>[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for CVE-[0m[1;36m2023[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m42503[0m[39m - BigDecimal DoS in TAR PAX Header Timestamp [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParsing[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe libFuzzer timeout is caused by a **denial of service vulnerability [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mCVE-[0m[1;36m2023[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m42503[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** in the `[0m[1;35mparseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.java`. The issue stems from:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Insufficient Input Validation**: The regex pattern [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN` at line [0m[1;36m222[0m[39m is defined as [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`-?\\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m19[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\\.\\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?`, which correctly limits the integer part to [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits but[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallows **unlimited decimal digits** through the `\\.\\d*` component.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Expensive BigDecimal Operations**: When a malicious input containing millions [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof decimal digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"1.000000...000"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is processed:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m creates a BigDecimal with extremely high scale[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m277[0m[39m's `[0m[1;35mremainder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBigDecimal.ONE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operation triggers the Knuth division [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm in BigInteger[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This results in computational complexity that can take hours instead of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmilliseconds[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Attack Vectors**: [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very long fractions [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m300[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m+ digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: [0m[32m"1.000000000000...000"[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exponent notation: [0m[32m"9e9999999"[0m[39m or [0m[32m"9E9999999"[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Asymmetry Between Read and Write**: The write side [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveOutputStream.addInstantPaxHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m254[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m explicitly limits [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision to [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal places using `[0m[1;35msetScale[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m, RoundingMode.DOWN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, but the read [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mside has no such limitation.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Implementation[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix: Update the Validation Pattern**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java` at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m222[0m[39m:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change from:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change to:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,18[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Update the comment** at lines [0m[1;36m216[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m219[0m[39m to reflect the decimal precision limit:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * PAX header timestamp format allows decimal seconds with optional fractional part[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * as per this definition: [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [4;94mhttps://pubs.opengroup.org/onlinepubs/9699919799/utilities/pax.html#tag_20_92_13_05[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <p>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * Since they are parsed into long values, maximum length of the integer part is [0m[1;36m19[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLong.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * The fractional part is limited to [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m digits to prevent denial of service attacks[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith BigDecimal operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee JDK-[0m[1;36m6560193[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * This provides precision far exceeding nanosecond requirements [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplaces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Sufficient Precision**: [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Nanosecond precision requires only [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal places[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The write side uses [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal places [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m254[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msetScale[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRoundingMode.DOWN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m decimal places provides more than adequate precision while preventing DoS[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Change**: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Single line modification to the regex pattern[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to parsing logic or algorithm[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lowest risk of introducing new bugs[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Prevents All Known Attack Vectors**:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Blocks inputs with millions of decimal digits[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pattern still rejects exponent notation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m or [0m[32m'E'[0m[39m allowed[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains compatibility with all legitimate timestamp values[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistency with Write Side**:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns read validation with write-side precision limits[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains symmetry between serialization and deserialization[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Functionality**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests remain valid [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey use [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal places[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test cases at lines [0m[1;36m260[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m281[0m[39m continue to verify rejection of invalid inputs[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Backward compatible with all legitimate TAR archives[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Truncation of extreme precision timestamps**: If a TAR archive contains [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimestamps with more than [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m decimal places, the pattern validation will reject [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem with an IOException.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is acceptable because:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Such timestamps are non-standard and likely malicious[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The write side never produces timestamps with more than [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal places[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m decimal places far exceeds any practical precision requirements[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The error message clearly indicates the issue: [0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mfield value is invalid"[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Breaking Changes**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All legitimate TAR archives will continue to parse correctly[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing unit tests will pass[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix is security-hardening that doesn't affect normal operation[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Locate [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Find line [0m[1;36m222[0m[39m containing the `PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN` definition[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace `[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\\.\\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?` with `[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\\.\\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m18[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?`[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Update the JavaDoc comment at lines [0m[1;36m216[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m219[0m[39m to document the decimal precision [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimit[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify that all existing tests pass, especially [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntryTest.testPaxTimeFieldsForInvalidValues[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Considered but Not Recommended[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn alternative approach would be to replace BigDecimal parsing with string [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanipulation:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Split the string at the decimal point[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Parse seconds and fractional parts separately[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Avoid BigDecimal entirely[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, this approach:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Requires more extensive code changes[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Increases risk of introducing bugs[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Doesn't provide significant additional benefit[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The pattern fix is sufficient and less invasive[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Verification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix can be verified by:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Running existing unit tests to ensure no regression[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Testing with malicious inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"1."[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m300[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m zeros[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify rejection[0m   [2m                [0m
